                      '\n'
                      '\n'
                      'def extract_afp_datetime(url):\n'
                      '    match = re.search(r"\\.([\\d]{8}T[\\d]{6})Z", url)\n'
                      '    if match:\n'
                      '        dt_str = match.group(1)\n'
                      '        dt_utc = datetime.strptime(dt_str, '
                      '"%Y%m%dT%H%M%S").replace(\n'
                      '            tzinfo=ZoneInfo("UTC")\n'
                      '        )\n'
                      '        dt_et = dt_utc.astimezone(ET_ZONE)\n'
                      '        return dt_et.strftime("%-m/%-d/%YT%H:%M:%S")  # '
                      'Example: 4/16/2025T13:03:21\n'
                      '    return None\n'
                      '\n'
                      '\n'
                      'with open(\n'
                      '    "personal_batched_csvs/Enriched_Links3.csv", "r", '

                      ') as outfile:\n'

                      '    writer = csv.writer(outfile)\n'

                             'GEMMA_TOK_PER_MIN = 15000\n'
                             '\n'
                             '\n'
                             '# Token estimator (roughly 4 chars/token)\n'
                             'def estimate_tokens(text):\n'
                             '    return max(1, len(text) // 4)\n'
                             '\n'
                             '\n'
                             '# Deques to hold (timestamp, token count)\n'
                             'llama_requests = deque()\n'
                             'llama_tokens = deque()\n'
                             '\n'
                             'gemma_requests = deque()\n'
                             'gemma_tokens = deque()\n'
                             '\n'
                             '\n'
                             'def throttle_model(requests_deque, tokens_deque, '
                             'max_req, max_tok, new_tok):\n'
                             '    now = time.time()\n'
                             '\n'
                             '    # Purge requests older than 60 seconds\n'
                             '    while requests_deque and now - '
                             'requests_deque[0] > 60:\n'
                             '        requests_deque.popleft()\n'
                             '    while tokens_deque and now - '
                             'tokens_deque[0][0] > 60:\n'
                             '        tokens_deque.popleft()\n'
                             '\n'
                             '    # Wait if we exceed limits\n'
                             '    while (\n'
                             '        len(requests_deque) >= max_req\n'
                             '        or sum(tok for _, tok in tokens_deque) + '
                             'new_tok > max_tok\n'
                             '    ):\n'
                             '        print("sleeping while groq models cool '
                             'down...")\n'
                             '        time.sleep(1)\n'
                             '        now = time.time()\n'
                             '        while requests_deque and now - '
                             'requests_deque[0] > 60:\n'
                             '            requests_deque.popleft()\n'
                             '        while tokens_deque and now - '
                             'tokens_deque[0][0] > 60:\n'
                             '            tokens_deque.popleft()\n'
                             '\n'
                             '    requests_deque.append(now)\n'
                             '    tokens_deque.append((now, new_tok))\n'
                             '\n'
                             '\n'
                             'representative_urls = []\n'
                             '\n'
                             'with open("txt_files/representative_links.txt", '

                             '    parsed_dict = groq_parse_url(url)\n'
                             '    while parsed_dict is None and tries > 0:\n'

 'get_all_files.py': 'import os\n'
                     'from pathlib import Path\n'
                     'import pprint  # Used for pretty-printing the output '
                     'dictionary\n'
                     '\n'
                     '\n'
                     'def get_file_contents_recursively(directory_path: str) '
                     '-> dict:\n'
                     '    """\n'
                     '    Recursively goes through each file in a directory '
                     'and its subdirectories\n'
                     '    and gets its text content.\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    Rules:\n'
                     "    - For files named 'Links.csv' or 'temp.txt', it "
                     'reads only the first 3 lines.\n'
                     '    - For all other files, it reads the entire content.\n'
                     '    - It ignores any files or directories that start '
                     "with a dot (e.g., '.git', '.DS_Store').\n"
                     "    - It ignores specific folders like '__pycache__' and "
                     "'.vscode'.\n"
                     '    - It skips files that cannot be decoded as text '
                     '(like images or binaries).\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    Args:\n'
                     '        directory_path: The path to the root directory '
                     'to scan.\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    Returns:\n'
                     '        A dictionary where keys are the relative file '
                     'paths (e.g.,\n'
                     "        'src/main.py') and values are the text "
                     'contents.\n'
                     '    """\n'
                     '    path = Path(directory_path)\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    if not path.is_dir():\n'
                     '        print(f"Error: The path \'{directory_path}\' is '
                     'not a valid directory.")\n'
                     '        return {}\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    file_contents = {}\n'
                     '    special_files = {\n'
                     '        "Links.csv",\n'
                     '        "temp.txt",\n'
                     '        "Enriched_Links_Updated.csv",\n'
                     '        "proxies_list.txt",\n'
                     '    }\n'
                     '    lines_to_read = 3\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    # --- NEW: Set of directory names to completely '
                     'ignore ---\n'
                     '    # Using a set provides fast lookups.\n'
                     '    ignored_dirs = {"__pycache__", ".vscode", ".git", '
                     '"node_modules"}\n'
                     '\n'
                     "    # Use path.rglob('*') to recursively find all items\n"
                     '    for item in path.rglob("*"):\n'
                     '        # Get the path relative to the starting '
                     'directory\n'
                     '        relative_item_path = item.relative_to(path)\n'
                     '\n'
                     '        # --- UPDATED LOGIC TO IGNORE HIDDEN AND '
                     'SPECIFIC FOLDERS ---\n'
                     '        # Check if any part of the path is in the '
                     "ignored_dirs set or starts with a '.'\n"
                     '        is_ignored = any(\n'
                     '            part in ignored_dirs or '
                     'part.startswith(".")\n'
                     '            for part in relative_item_path.parts\n'
                     '        )\n'
                     '\n'
                     '        if is_ignored:\n'
                     '            continue  # Skip to the next item in the '
                     'loop\n'
                     '\n'
                     '        # Ensure we are only processing files from here '
                     'on\n'
                     '        if item.is_file():\n'
                     '            # Use forward slashes for cross-platform '
                     'consistency in keys\n'
                     '            relative_path_key = '
                     'str(relative_item_path).replace("\\\\", "/")\n'
                     '\n'
                     '            try:\n'
                     '                with open(item, "r", encoding="utf-8", '
                     'errors="ignore") as f:\n'
                     '                    if item.name in special_files:\n'
                     '                        lines = [next(f) for _ in '
                     'range(lines_to_read)]\n'
                     '                        content = "".join(lines)\n'
                     '                        print(\n'
                     '                            f"-> Reading first '
                     '{lines_to_read} lines from \'{relative_path_key}\'..."\n'
                     '                        )\n'
                     '                    else:\n'
                     '                        content = f.read()\n'
                     '\n'
                     '                    file_contents[relative_path_key] = '
                     'content\n'
                     '\n'
                     '            except StopIteration:\n'
                     '                file_contents[relative_path_key] = '
                     'content\n'
                     '            except Exception as e:\n'
                     '                print(\n'
                     '                    f"Warning: Could not read '
                     "'{relative_path_key}' due to an error: {e}. "
                     'Skipping."\n'
                     '                )\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    return file_contents\n'
                     '\n'
                     '\n'
                     '# --- Main execution block ---\n'
                     'if __name__ == "__main__":\n'
                     '    target_directory = "."\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    import sys\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    if len(sys.argv) > 1:\n'
                     '        target_directory = sys.argv[1]\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    print(\n'
                     '        f"Recursively scanning for text files in: '
                     '\'{os.path.abspath(target_directory)}\'\\n"\n'
                     '    )\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    all_contents = '
                     'get_file_contents_recursively(target_directory)\n'
                     '\n'
                     '    if all_contents:\n'
                     '        print("\\n--- File Contents Found ---")\n'
                     '        pprint.pprint(all_contents)\n'
                     '    else:\n'
                     '        print(\n'
                     '            "No readable text files or directories were '
                     'found after applying ignore rules."\n'
                     '        )\n',

                      'from utils.llm_utils import ArticleInfo, '
                      'gemini_parse_web_content\n'
                      'from batch_website_scraper import call_groq, '
                      'get_naughty_links\n'
                      'from utils.json_ld_finder import '
                      'extract_ld_json_and_article\n'
                      'from config import GEMINI_MODEL, CHAR_LIMIT\n'
                      'from bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n'
                      'from utils.scraping_utils import scrape_site, '
                      'remove_paths_and_urls\n'
                      '\n'
                      '\n'
                      'def scrape_link(url: str, writer):\n'
                      '    naughties = get_naughty_links()\n'
                      '    for naughty in naughties:\n'
                      '        if naughty in url:\n'
                      '            call_groq(writer=writer, url=url)\n'
                      '    else:\n'
                      '        try:\n'
                      '            llm = GEMINI_MODEL\n'
                      '            print("link passed the vibe check")\n'
                      '            html = scrape_site(url)\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            json_ld_try = '
                      'extract_ld_json_and_article(soup)\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            # Remove noisy elements to reduce token '
                      'count\n'
                      '            for tag in soup(\n'
                      '                [\n'
                      '                    "script",\n'
                      '                    "style",\n'
                      '                    "nav",\n'
                      '                    "footer",\n'
                      '                    "aside",\n'
                      '                    "noscript",\n'
                      '                    "iframe",\n'
                      '                    "link",\n'
                      '                    "picture",\n'
                      '                    "source",\n'
                      '                    "img",\n'
                      '                ]\n'
                      '            ):\n'
                      '                tag.decompose()\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            # Optionally keep only relevant top-level '
                      'sections (e.g. <article>, <main>, etc.)\n'
                      '            main_content = soup.find("article") or '
                      'soup.find("main") or soup.body\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            # If found, keep only the main content; '
                      'else fallback to the cleaned soup\n'
                      '            if main_content:\n'
                      '                cleaned_html = str(main_content)\n'
                      '            else:\n'
                      '                cleaned_html = str(soup)\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            pass_dict = {"URL": url}\n'
                      '            if json_ld_try is not None:\n'
                      '                pass_dict["json_ld"] = json_ld_try\n'
                      '            pass_dict["website_content"] = '
                      'cleaned_html\n'
                      '\n'
                      '            token_est = len(str(pass_dict)) / 4\n'

                      '                [\n'

                      '                    parsed_dict.authors,\n'

                      '                    parsed_dict.published_date,\n'
                      '                    parsed_dict.modified_date,\n'
                      '                    llm,\n'
                      '                ]\n'
                      '            )\n'
                      '        except Exception as e:\n'
                      '            print(f"Error fetching {url}: {e}")\n'
                      '            print("calling groq")\n'
                      '            call_groq(writer=writer, url=url)\n'
                      '\n'
                      '\n'
                      'def process_and_enrich_csv(\n'
                      '    '
                      'input_path="personal_batched_csvs/Enriched_Links2.csv",\n'
                      '    '
                      'output_path="personal_batched_csvs/Enriched_Links3.csv",\n'
                      '):\n'
                      '    """\n'
                      '    Reads input CSV and writes a new CSV with enriched '
                      'data:\n'
                      '    - Healthy rows are copied as-is.\n'
                      '    - Lonely rows are processed using '
                      '`scrape_link(url)` and replaced.\n'
                      '    """\n'
                      '\n'
                      '    def try_open(encoding):\n'
                      '        with open(\n'
                      '            input_path, newline="", encoding=encoding, '
                      'errors="replace"\n'
                      '        ) as infile, open(output_path, "w", newline="", '
                      'encoding="utf-8") as outfile:\n'
                      '            reader = csv.reader(infile)\n'
                      '            writer = csv.writer(outfile)\n'
                      '            for row in reader:\n'
                      '                # If the row is completely empty, write '
                      'it as-is\n'
                      '                if not any(cell.strip() for cell in '
                      'row):\n'
                      '                    writer.writerow(row)\n'
                      '                # Lonely row: first cell has data, rest '
                      'are empty\n'
                      '                elif row[0].strip() and '
                      'all(cell.strip() == "" for cell in row[1:]):\n'
                      '                    scrape_link(url=row[0].strip(), '
                      'writer=writer)\n'
                      '                else:\n'
                      '                    writer.writerow(row)\n'
                      '\n'
                      '    try:\n'
                      '        try_open("utf-8")\n'
                      '    except UnicodeDecodeError:\n'
                      '        try_open("ISO-8859-1")\n'
                      '\n'
                      '\n'
                      'process_and_enrich_csv()\n',

                          'Field Descriptions:\n'
                          'title (str): The headline or main title of the '
                          'article, as shown on the page. This should match '
                          "what a reader would consider the article's title.\n"
                          '\n'
                          'authors (str): The full name(s) of the '

                          '\n'

                          '"Reuters").\n'
                          '\n'

                          'is Z (zulu), in a time stamp like this: '

                          'modified_date (str): The last modified or updated '

                          'is no update time, return the same value as '
                          'published_date.\n'
                          '\n'
                          'Instructions:\n'
                          'Look first in structured data (json ld, OpenGraph '
                          'tags, and meta tags).\n'
                          '\n'
                          'If structured data is missing or incomplete, fall '

                            '    cleaned_article_text = '

                         'def dump_proxies():\n'
                         '\n'
                         '    regex = r"[0-9]+(?:\\.[0-9]+){3}:[0-9]+"\n'

                         '    test_str = c.text\n'

                         '    with open("proxies_list.txt", "w") as file:\n'
                         '        for i in a:\n'
                         '            print(i.group(), file=file)\n'
                         '\n'
                         '    d = '
                         'requests.get("https://free-proxy-list.net/")\n'
                         '    soup = BeautifulSoup(d.content, "html.parser")\n'
                         '    td_elements = soup.select(".fpl-list .table '
                         'tbody tr td")\n'
                         '    ips = []\n'
                         '    ports = []\n'
                         '    for j in range(0, len(td_elements), 8):\n'
                         '        ips.append(td_elements[j].text.strip())\n'
                         '        ports.append(td_elements[j + '
                         '1].text.strip())\n'

                         '            proxy = f"{ip}:{port}"\n'

                         '    return proxy_list\n',

                            '\n'
                            'def remove_paths_and_urls(html_string: str) -> '
                            'str:\n'
                            '    """\n'
                            "    Uses regex to remove '<div', '<span', URLs, "
                            'and common file path patterns\n'
                            '    (case-insensitive for tags).\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    WARNING: This is a brittle approach using '
                            'regex directly on HTML. It will\n'
                            '             likely result in invalid/broken HTML '
                            'structure and may remove\n'
                            '             unintended text that resembles a URL '
                            'or path. Use with caution.\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    Args:\n'
                            '        html_string: The HTML content as a '
                            'string.\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    Returns:\n'
                            '        The modified string.\n'
                            '    """\n'
                            '    # 1. Pattern for URLs/URIs (common web '
                            'protocols, protocol-relative, www.)\n'
                            '    # Designed to match typical structures found '
                            'in attributes like href or src.\n'
                            '    url_patterns = r"""\n'
                            '        '
                            '(?:https?|ftp|file):\\/\\/[\\-A-Z0-9+&@#\\/%?=~_|!:,.;]*[\\-A-Z0-9+&@#\\/%=~_|]  '
                            '# http, https, ftp, file\n'
                            '        |\n'
                            '        \\/\\/[^\\s<>"\']+  # Protocol-relative '
                            '//...\n'
                            '        |\n'
                            '        (?<!\\w)www\\.[^\\s<>"\']+ # www. links '
                            '(negative lookbehind to avoid matching things '
                            "like 'abcwww.')\n"
                            '    """\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    # 2. Pattern for common file paths '
                            '(Unix/Windows style, relative/absolute)\n'
                            '    # Matches starting patterns like /, ./, ../, '
                            'C:\\ followed by typical path characters.\n'
                            '    path_patterns = r"""\n'
                            '        '
                            '(?:[a-zA-Z]:\\\\|\\.\\.?[\\\\\\/]|\\/)[a-zA-Z0-9\\/\\\\._-]+ '
                            '# Drive paths, relative paths, absolute paths\n'
                            '    """\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    # Combine patterns with OR (|). Order: URLs, '
                            'Paths, Tags. Use verbose regex for readability.\n'
                            '    combined_pattern = re.compile(\n'
                            '        f"({url_patterns})|({path_patterns})",\n'
                            '        re.IGNORECASE | re.VERBOSE,\n'
                            '    )\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    # Perform the substitution, replacing any '
                            'match with an empty string\n'
                            '    cleaned_html = combined_pattern.sub("", '
                            'html_string)\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    return cleaned_html\n'
                            '\n'
                            '\n'
                            'def scrape_site(url, proxies=None, '
                            'max_retries=3):\n'
                            '    proxies = proxies.copy() if proxies else []\n'
                            '    for attempt in range(1, max_retries + 1):\n'
                            '        proxy = random.choice(proxies) if proxies '
                            'else None\n'
                            '\n'
                            '        try:\n'
                            '            with sync_playwright() as p:\n'
                            '                ua = random.choice(USER_AGENTS)\n'
                            '                vp = random.choice(VIEWPORTS)\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                browser = p.chromium.launch(\n'
                            '                    headless=True,\n'
                            '                    '
                            'args=["--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled"],\n'
                            '                )\n'
                            '                ctx_args = {\n'
                            '                    "user_agent": ua,\n'
                            '                    "viewport": vp,\n'
                            '                    "locale": "en-US",\n'
                            '                    "timezone_id": '
                            '"America/Los_Angeles",\n'
                            '                    "extra_http_headers": '
                            'EXTRA_HEADERS,\n'
                            '                }\n'
                            '                if proxy:\n'
                            '                    ctx_args["proxy"] = proxy\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                context = '
                            'browser.new_context(**ctx_args)\n'
                            '                stealth_sync(context)\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                page = context.new_page()\n'
                            '                page.set_default_timeout(10000)  '
                            '# 10s\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                # Block non-HTML assets for speed '
                            'and minimal fingerprint\n'
                            '                def _block_assets(route: Route):\n'
                            '                    if '
                            'route.request.resource_type in (\n'
                            '                        "image",\n'
                            '                        "stylesheet",\n'
                            '                        "font",\n'
                            '                        "media",\n'
                            '                    ):\n'
                            '                        return route.abort()\n'
                            '                    return route.continue_()\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                page.route("**/*", '
                            '_block_assets)\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                # Faster load event: '
                            'DOMContentLoaded\n'
                            '                response = page.goto(url)  # , '
                            'wait_until="domcontentloaded")\n'
                            '                if not response or '
                            'response.status != 200:\n'
                            '                    raise Exception(\n'
                            '                        f"Bad status: '
                            "{response.status if response else 'no "
                            'response\'}"\n'
                            '                    )\n'
                            '\n'
                            '                # --- CHANGE HERE ---\n'
                            '                # Get the raw response body as '
                            'bytes instead of letting\n'
                            '                # Playwright decode it into a '
                            'string.\n'
                            '                html = page.content()\n'
                            '                browser.close()\n'
                            '                return html\n'
                            '\n'
                            '        except Exception as e:\n'
                            '            msg = str(e)\n'
                            '            print(f"[Attempt '
                            '{attempt}/{max_retries}] {msg}")\n'
                            '\n'
                            '            # drop unusable proxy\n'
                            '            if proxy and '
                            '"ERR_PROXY_CONNECTION_FAILED" in msg:\n'
                            '                print(f"Dropping bad proxy: '
                            '{proxy[\'server\']}")\n'
                            '                proxies.remove(proxy)\n'
                            '\n'
                            '            time.sleep(2**attempt * 0.5 + '
                            'random.random())\n'
                            '\n'
                            '    raise RuntimeError(f"Failed to scrape {url} '
                            'after {max_retries} attempts")\n'
                            '\n'
                            '\n'
                            'def fix_mojibake(text: str) -> str:\n'
                            '    """\n'
                            '    Attempts to fix common mojibake issues where '
                            'UTF-8 text was\n'
                            '    incorrectly decoded as latin-1 or a similar '
                            'encoding.\n'
                            '    """\n'
                            '    if not isinstance(text, str):\n'
                            '        return text\n'
                            '    try:\n'
                            '        # This sequence reverses the common '
                            'error:\n'
                            '        # 1. Encode the wrongly-decoded string '
                            'back into bytes using the assumed incorrect '
                            'encoding (latin-1).\n'
                            '        # 2. Decode those bytes correctly as '
                            'UTF-8.\n'
                            '        return '
                            'text.encode("latin-1").decode("utf-8")\n'
                            '    except (UnicodeEncodeError, '
                            'UnicodeDecodeError):\n'
                            '        # If it fails, the string was not '
                            'mojibake, so return it as-is.\n'
                            '        return text\n',
 'utils/text_scrubber.py': 'import re\n'
                           '\n'
                           'def scrub_text(raw_text: str) -> str:\n'
                           "    # Step 1: Unescape characters like \\' and "
                           '\\n\n'
                           '    text = '
                           "raw_text.encode('utf-8').decode('unicode_escape')\n"
                           '\n'
                           '    # Step 2: Remove newlines followed by many '
                           'spaces (layout artifacts)\n'
                           "    text = re.sub(r'\\n\\s+', ' ', text)\n"
                           '\n'
                           '    # Step 3: Remove remaining newlines\n'
                           "    text = re.sub(r'\\n+', ' ', text)\n"
                           '\n'
                           '    # Step 4: Collapse multiple spaces\n'
                           "    text = re.sub(r'\\s{2,}', ' ', text).strip()\n"
                           '\n'
                           '    return text\n'}
